## Guides
*An awesome list of Swift related guides.* 

### Newsletter
[back to top](#readme) 

* [Swift Developments](https://andybargh.com/swiftdevelopments/) - A weekly curated newsletter containing for people interested in designing and developing their own iOS, watchOS and Apple TV apps.
* [Swift Weekly Brief](https://swiftweeklybrief.com/) - A multi author curated newsletter.

### Official Guides
[back to top](#readme) 

* [API Design Guidelines](https://www.swift.org/documentation/api-design-guidelines/) - Official Swift API design guidelines.
* [Apple eBook](https://books.apple.com/us/book/the-swift-programming-language-swift-5-5/id881256329) - Official Apple eBook for Swift beginners.
* [Getting Started](https://www.swift.org/getting-started/) - Find information about the how to use the Swift programming language.
* [Introducing SwiftUI](https://developer.apple.com/tutorials/swiftui) - Official SwiftUI tutorial with 4+ hours of content and interactive tutorials.

### Style Guides
[back to top](#readme) 

* [Airbnb](https://github.com/airbnb/swift) - Airbnb's Official Style Guide.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/airbnb/swift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/airbnb/swift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/airbnb/swift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/airbnb/swift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/airbnb/swift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/airbnb/swift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/airbnb/swift)

* [Google](https://google.github.io/swift/) - This style guide is based on Apple’s excellent Swift standard library style and also incorporates feedback from usage across multiple Swift projects within Google.
* [LinkedIn](https://github.com/linkedin/swift-style-guide) - LinkedIn's Official Style Guide.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/linkedin/swift-style-guide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/linkedin/swift-style-guide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/linkedin/swift-style-guide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/linkedin/swift-style-guide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/linkedin/swift-style-guide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/linkedin/swift-style-guide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/linkedin/swift-style-guide)

* [Raywenderlich](https://github.com/raywenderlich/swift-style-guide) - Raywenderlich guide, a must read.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/raywenderlich/swift-style-guide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/raywenderlich/swift-style-guide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/raywenderlich/swift-style-guide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/raywenderlich/swift-style-guide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/raywenderlich/swift-style-guide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/raywenderlich/swift-style-guide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/raywenderlich/swift-style-guide)


### Third party Guides
[back to top](#readme) 

* [30 Days of Swift](https://github.com/allenwong/30DaysofSwift) - A cool 30 days tutorial.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/allenwong/30DaysofSwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/allenwong/30DaysofSwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/allenwong/30DaysofSwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/allenwong/30DaysofSwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/allenwong/30DaysofSwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/allenwong/30DaysofSwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/allenwong/30DaysofSwift)

* [About Swift](https://github.com/NicolaLancellotti-About/About-Swift) - A playground about the Swift language.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/NicolaLancellotti-About/About-Swift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/NicolaLancellotti-About/About-Swift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/NicolaLancellotti-About/About-Swift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/NicolaLancellotti-About/About-Swift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/NicolaLancellotti-About/About-Swift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/NicolaLancellotti-About/About-Swift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/NicolaLancellotti-About/About-Swift)

* [Awesome Swift Education](https://github.com/hsavit1/Awesome-Swift-Education) - An organized list of essential Swift Language Topics.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hsavit1/Awesome-Swift-Education) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/hsavit1/Awesome-Swift-Education) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/hsavit1/Awesome-Swift-Education) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/hsavit1/Awesome-Swift-Education) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/hsavit1/Awesome-Swift-Education) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/hsavit1/Awesome-Swift-Education) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/hsavit1/Awesome-Swift-Education)

* [Conferences.digital](https://github.com/zagahr/Conferences.digital) - Watch conference videos in a native macOS app.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zagahr/Conferences.digital) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/zagahr/Conferences.digital) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/zagahr/Conferences.digital) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/zagahr/Conferences.digital) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/zagahr/Conferences.digital) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/zagahr/Conferences.digital) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/zagahr/Conferences.digital)

* [Developing iOS Apps with Swift](https://podcasts.apple.com/us/podcast/developing-ios-11-apps-with-swift/id1315130780) - Stanford course by Paul Hegarty.
* [Hacking With Swift](https://www.hackingwithswift.com) - Complete training course that teaches app development through 30 hands-on projects, for free.
* [Ray Wenderlich Tutorials, Videos, Podcasts and books](https://www.raywenderlich.com) - High quality programming tutorials.
* [Swift Education](https://github.com/swifteducation) - A community of educators sharing materials for teaching Swift and app development.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/swifteducation) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/swifteducation) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/swifteducation) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/swifteducation) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/swifteducation) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/swifteducation) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/swifteducation)

* [swift-tips](https://github.com/vincent-pradeilles/swift-tips) - A series of useful tips by Vincent Pradeilles.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vincent-pradeilles/swift-tips) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/vincent-pradeilles/swift-tips) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/vincent-pradeilles/swift-tips) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/vincent-pradeilles/swift-tips) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/vincent-pradeilles/swift-tips) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/vincent-pradeilles/swift-tips) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/vincent-pradeilles/swift-tips)

* [SwiftDoc](https://swiftdoc.org/) - Auto-generated documentation.
* [SwiftGuide CN](https://github.com/ipader/SwiftGuide) - A Chinese written guide.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ipader/SwiftGuide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ipader/SwiftGuide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/ipader/SwiftGuide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/ipader/SwiftGuide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/ipader/SwiftGuide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/ipader/SwiftGuide) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/ipader/SwiftGuide)

* [SwiftTips](https://github.com/JohnSundell/SwiftTips) - A collection of useful tips by John Sundell.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/JohnSundell/SwiftTips) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/JohnSundell/SwiftTips) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/JohnSundell/SwiftTips) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/JohnSundell/SwiftTips) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/JohnSundell/SwiftTips) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/JohnSundell/SwiftTips) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/JohnSundell/SwiftTips)

* [The Swift Web Developer](https://theswiftwebdeveloper.com) - A publication for Swift Web Developers.
* [whats-new-in-swift-4](https://github.com/ole/whats-new-in-swift-4) - An Xcode playground showcasing the new features in Swift 4.0.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ole/whats-new-in-swift-4) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ole/whats-new-in-swift-4) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/ole/whats-new-in-swift-4) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/ole/whats-new-in-swift-4) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/ole/whats-new-in-swift-4) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/ole/whats-new-in-swift-4) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/ole/whats-new-in-swift-4)


## Boilerplates

* [iOS project template](https://github.com/messeb/ios-project-template) - iOS project template with fastlane lanes, Travis CI jobs and GitHub integrations of Codecov, HoundCI for SwiftLint and Danger.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/messeb/ios-project-template) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/messeb/ios-project-template) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/messeb/ios-project-template) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/messeb/ios-project-template) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/messeb/ios-project-template) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/messeb/ios-project-template) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/messeb/ios-project-template)

* [Swift Module Template](https://github.com/fulldecent/swift5-module-template) - An opinionated starting point for awesome, reusable modules.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fulldecent/swift5-module-template) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/fulldecent/swift5-module-template) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/fulldecent/swift5-module-template) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/fulldecent/swift5-module-template) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/fulldecent/swift5-module-template) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/fulldecent/swift5-module-template) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/fulldecent/swift5-module-template)

* [Online Swift Playground](http://online.swiftplayground.run) - Online Swift Playground.

## Editor Support

### Emacs
[back to top](#readme)

## Benchmark

* [xcprofiler](https://github.com/giginet/xcprofiler) - Command line utility to profile compilation time.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/giginet/xcprofiler) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/giginet/xcprofiler) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/giginet/xcprofiler) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/giginet/xcprofiler) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/giginet/xcprofiler) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/giginet/xcprofiler) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/giginet/xcprofiler)


## Converters

* [Swiftify](https://swiftify.com/#/converter/code/) - Objective-C to Swift online code converter and Xcode extension.
* [Zolang](https://github.com/Zolang/Zolang) :penguin: - A DSL for generating code in multiple programming languages.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Zolang/Zolang) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Zolang/Zolang) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/Zolang/Zolang) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/Zolang/Zolang) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/Zolang/Zolang) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Zolang/Zolang) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/Zolang/Zolang)

## Dependency Managers
*Dependency manager software for Swift.* 
* [Accio](https://github.com/JamitLabs/Accio) - A SwiftPM based dependency manager for iOS & Co. with improvements over Carthage.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/JamitLabs/Accio) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/JamitLabs/Accio) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/JamitLabs/Accio) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/JamitLabs/Accio) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/JamitLabs/Accio) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/JamitLabs/Accio) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/JamitLabs/Accio)

* [Carthage](https://github.com/Carthage/Carthage) - A new dependency manager.

## Patterns

### App Routing
*Internal app routing systems.* [back to top](#readme) 

* [Appz](https://github.com/SwiftKitz/Appz) - Launch external apps and deeplink with ease.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SwiftKitz/Appz) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/SwiftKitz/Appz) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/SwiftKitz/Appz) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/SwiftKitz/Appz) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/SwiftKitz/Appz) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/SwiftKitz/Appz) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/SwiftKitz/Appz)

* [Crossroad](https://github.com/giginet/Crossroad) - :oncoming_bus: Crossroad is an URL router focused on handling Custom URL Schemes.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/giginet/Crossroad) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/giginet/Crossroad) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/giginet/Crossroad) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/giginet/Crossroad) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/giginet/Crossroad) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/giginet/Crossroad) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/giginet/Crossroad)

* [LightRoute](https://github.com/SpectralDragon/LiteRoute) - Routing between VIPER modules.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SpectralDragon/LiteRoute) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/SpectralDragon/LiteRoute) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/SpectralDragon/LiteRoute) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/SpectralDragon/LiteRoute) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/SpectralDragon/LiteRoute) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/SpectralDragon/LiteRoute) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/SpectralDragon/LiteRoute)

* [Linker](https://github.com/MaksimKurpa/Linker) - Lightweight way to handle internal and external deeplinks for iOS.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MaksimKurpa/Linker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/MaksimKurpa/Linker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/MaksimKurpa/Linker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/MaksimKurpa/Linker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/MaksimKurpa/Linker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/MaksimKurpa/Linker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/MaksimKurpa/Linker)

* [MonarchRouter](https://github.com/nikans/MonarchRouter) - Declarative state- and URL-based router. Complex automatic View Controllers hierarchy transitions. Time-tested server-side conventions.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nikans/MonarchRouter) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/nikans/MonarchRouter) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/nikans/MonarchRouter) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/nikans/MonarchRouter) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/nikans/MonarchRouter) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/nikans/MonarchRouter) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/nikans/MonarchRouter)

* [RxFlow](https://github.com/RxSwiftCommunity/RxFlow) - RxFlow is a navigation framework for iOS applications based on a Reactive Flow Coordinator pattern.

### Concurrency
*Easier ways to work with concurrency.* [back to top](#readme) 

* [async+](https://github.com/async-plus/async-plus) :penguin: - A chainable interface for Swift 5.5's async/await.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/async-plus/async-plus) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/async-plus/async-plus) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/async-plus/async-plus) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/async-plus/async-plus) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/async-plus/async-plus) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/async-plus/async-plus) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/async-plus/async-plus)

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AsyncNinja/AsyncNinja) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/AsyncNinja/AsyncNinja) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/AsyncNinja/AsyncNinja) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/AsyncNinja/AsyncNinja) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/AsyncNinja/AsyncNinja) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/AsyncNinja/AsyncNinja) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/AsyncNinja/AsyncNinja)

* [Futures](https://github.com/davidask/Futures) :penguin: - Lightweight promises for iOS, macOS, tvOS, watchOS, and server-side.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/davidask/Futures) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/davidask/Futures) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/davidask/Futures) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/davidask/Futures) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/davidask/Futures) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/davidask/Futures) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/davidask/Futures)

* [GroupWork](https://github.com/quanvo87/GroupWork) :penguin: - Easy concurrent, asynchronous tasks.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/quanvo87/GroupWork) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/quanvo87/GroupWork) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/quanvo87/GroupWork) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/quanvo87/GroupWork) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/quanvo87/GroupWork) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/quanvo87/GroupWork) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/quanvo87/GroupWork)

* [Kommander](https://github.com/intelygenz/Kommander-iOS) - Manage the task execution in different threads through Kommands.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/intelygenz/Kommander-iOS) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/intelygenz/Kommander-iOS) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/intelygenz/Kommander-iOS) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/intelygenz/Kommander-iOS) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/intelygenz/Kommander-iOS) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/intelygenz/Kommander-iOS) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/intelygenz/Kommander-iOS)

* [Queuer](https://github.com/FabrizioBrancati/Queuer) :penguin: - A queue manager, built on top of OperationQueue and Dispatch (aka GCD).

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/FabrizioBrancati/Queuer) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/FabrizioBrancati/Queuer) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/FabrizioBrancati/Queuer) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/FabrizioBrancati/Queuer) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/FabrizioBrancati/Queuer) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/FabrizioBrancati/Queuer) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/FabrizioBrancati/Queuer)

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/boraseoksoon/Throttler) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/boraseoksoon/Throttler) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/boraseoksoon/Throttler) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/boraseoksoon/Throttler) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/boraseoksoon/Throttler) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/boraseoksoon/Throttler) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/boraseoksoon/Throttler)

#### Core Data

* [AERecord](https://github.com/tadija/AERecord) - Super awesome Core Data wrapper library for iOS.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tadija/AERecord) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/tadija/AERecord) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/tadija/AERecord) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/tadija/AERecord) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/tadija/AERecord) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/tadija/AERecord) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/tadija/AERecord)

#### JSON
*Struggling using json data? Here are some interesting ways to handle it.* [back to top](#readme) 

* [AlamofireObjectMapper](https://github.com/tristanhimmelman/AlamofireObjectMapper) - An Alamofire extension which converts JSON response data into objects using ObjectMapper.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tristanhimmelman/AlamofireObjectMapper) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/tristanhimmelman/AlamofireObjectMapper) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/tristanhimmelman/AlamofireObjectMapper) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/tristanhimmelman/AlamofireObjectMapper) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/tristanhimmelman/AlamofireObjectMapper) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/tristanhimmelman/AlamofireObjectMapper) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/tristanhimmelman/AlamofireObjectMapper)

* [Alembic](https://github.com/ra1028/Alembic) - Functional JSON parsing, mapping to objects, and serialize to JSON.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ra1028/Alembic) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ra1028/Alembic) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/ra1028/Alembic) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/ra1028/Alembic) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/ra1028/Alembic) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/ra1028/Alembic) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/ra1028/Alembic)

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thoughtbot/Argo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/thoughtbot/Argo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/thoughtbot/Argo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/thoughtbot/Argo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/thoughtbot/Argo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/thoughtbot/Argo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/thoughtbot/Argo)

* [Arrow](https://github.com/freshOS/Arrow) - Elegant JSON Parsing.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/freshOS/Arrow) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/freshOS/Arrow) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/freshOS/Arrow) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/freshOS/Arrow) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/freshOS/Arrow) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/freshOS/Arrow) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/freshOS/Arrow)

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Anviking/Decodable) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Anviking/Decodable) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/Anviking/Decodable) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/Anviking/Decodable) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/Anviking/Decodable) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Anviking/Decodable) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/Anviking/Decodable)

* [Elevate](https://github.com/Nike-Inc/Elevate) - JSON parsing framework that makes parsing simple, reliable and composable.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Nike-Inc/Elevate) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Nike-Inc/Elevate) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/Nike-Inc/Elevate) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/Nike-Inc/Elevate) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/Nike-Inc/Elevate) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Nike-Inc/Elevate) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/Nike-Inc/Elevate)

* [EVReflection](https://github.com/evermeer/EVReflection) - Reflection based JSON encoding and decoding. Including support for NSDictionary, NSCoding, Printable, Hashable and Equatable.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/evermeer/EVReflection) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/evermeer/EVReflection) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/evermeer/EVReflection) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/evermeer/EVReflection) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/evermeer/EVReflection) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/evermeer/EVReflection) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/evermeer/EVReflection)

### Dependency Injection
*Dependency injection libs* [back to top](#readme) 

* [Cleanse](https://github.com/square/Cleanse) - A Lightweight Dependency Injection Framework by Square.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/square/Cleanse) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/square/Cleanse) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/square/Cleanse) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/square/Cleanse) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/square/Cleanse) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/square/Cleanse) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/square/Cleanse)

* [Corridor](https://github.com/symentis/Corridor) - A Coreader-like Dependency Injection μFramework.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/symentis/Corridor) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/symentis/Corridor) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/symentis/Corridor) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/symentis/Corridor) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/symentis/Corridor) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/symentis/Corridor) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/symentis/Corridor)

* [Deli](https://github.com/kawoou/Deli) - Deli is an easy-to-use Dependency Injection(DI).

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kawoou/Deli) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/kawoou/Deli) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/kawoou/Deli) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/kawoou/Deli) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/kawoou/Deli) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/kawoou/Deli) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/kawoou/Deli)

* [DIKit](https://github.com/Liftric/DIKit) - Dependency Injection Framework for Swift, inspired by KOIN.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Liftric/DIKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Liftric/DIKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/Liftric/DIKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/Liftric/DIKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/Liftric/DIKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Liftric/DIKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/Liftric/DIKit)

* [Dip](https://github.com/AliSoftware/Dip) - A simple Dependency Injection Container.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AliSoftware/Dip) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/AliSoftware/Dip) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/AliSoftware/Dip) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/AliSoftware/Dip) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/AliSoftware/Dip) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/AliSoftware/Dip) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/AliSoftware/Dip)

* [DITranquillity](https://github.com/ivlevAstef/DITranquillity/) - Dependency injection framework with tranquility.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ivlevAstef/DITranquillity/) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ivlevAstef/DITranquillity/) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/ivlevAstef/DITranquillity/) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/ivlevAstef/DITranquillity/) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/ivlevAstef/DITranquillity/) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/ivlevAstef/DITranquillity/) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/ivlevAstef/DITranquillity/)

* [Locatable](https://github.com/vincent-pradeilles/locatable) - A micro-framework that leverages Property Wrappers to implement the Service Locator pattern.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vincent-pradeilles/locatable) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/vincent-pradeilles/locatable) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/vincent-pradeilles/locatable) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/vincent-pradeilles/locatable) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/vincent-pradeilles/locatable) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/vincent-pradeilles/locatable) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/vincent-pradeilles/locatable)

* [Pure](https://github.com/devxoul/Pure) - A way to do a dependency injection without a DI container.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/devxoul/Pure) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/devxoul/Pure) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/devxoul/Pure) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/devxoul/Pure) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/devxoul/Pure) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/devxoul/Pure) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/devxoul/Pure)

* [Swinject](https://github.com/Swinject/Swinject) - A dependency injection framework.

##### Barcode

### Keyboard
*Do you want to create your own customized keyboard? Here are some interesting resources* [back to top](#readme) 

* [IHKeyboardAvoiding](https://github.com/IdleHandsApps/IHKeyboardAvoiding) - An elegant solution for keeping any UIView visible when the keyboard is being shown. No UIScrollView required.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/IdleHandsApps/IHKeyboardAvoiding) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/IdleHandsApps/IHKeyboardAvoiding) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/IdleHandsApps/IHKeyboardAvoiding) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/IdleHandsApps/IHKeyboardAvoiding) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/IdleHandsApps/IHKeyboardAvoiding) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/IdleHandsApps/IHKeyboardAvoiding) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/IdleHandsApps/IHKeyboardAvoiding)

* [IQKeyboardManager](https://github.com/hackiftekhar/IQKeyboardManager) - Codeless drop-in universal library allows to prevent issues of keyboard sliding up and cover UITextField/UITextView.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hackiftekhar/IQKeyboardManager) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/hackiftekhar/IQKeyboardManager) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/hackiftekhar/IQKeyboardManager) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/hackiftekhar/IQKeyboardManager) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/hackiftekhar/IQKeyboardManager) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/hackiftekhar/IQKeyboardManager) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/hackiftekhar/IQKeyboardManager)

* [KeyboardHideManager](https://github.com/bonyadmitr/KeyboardHideManager) - Codeless manager to hide keyboard by tapping on views for iOS.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bonyadmitr/KeyboardHideManager) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/bonyadmitr/KeyboardHideManager) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/bonyadmitr/KeyboardHideManager) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/bonyadmitr/KeyboardHideManager) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/bonyadmitr/KeyboardHideManager) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/bonyadmitr/KeyboardHideManager) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/bonyadmitr/KeyboardHideManager)

* [KeyboardShortcuts](https://github.com/sindresorhus/KeyboardShortcuts) - Add user-customizable global keyboard shortcuts to your macOS app. Includes a Cocoa and SwiftUI component.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sindresorhus/KeyboardShortcuts) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/sindresorhus/KeyboardShortcuts) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/sindresorhus/KeyboardShortcuts) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/sindresorhus/KeyboardShortcuts) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/sindresorhus/KeyboardShortcuts) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/sindresorhus/KeyboardShortcuts) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/sindresorhus/KeyboardShortcuts)

* [Ribbon](https://github.com/chriszielinski/Ribbon) - 🎀 A simple cross-platform toolbar/custom input accessory view library for iOS & macOS.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chriszielinski/Ribbon) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/chriszielinski/Ribbon) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/chriszielinski/Ribbon) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/chriszielinski/Ribbon) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/chriszielinski/Ribbon) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/chriszielinski/Ribbon) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/chriszielinski/Ribbon)

* [Typist](https://github.com/totocaster/Typist) - Small, drop-in UIKit keyboard manager for iOS apps-helps manage keyboard's screen presence and behavior without notification center.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/totocaster/Typist) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/totocaster/Typist) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/totocaster/Typist) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/totocaster/Typist) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/totocaster/Typist) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/totocaster/Typist) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/totocaster/Typist)

### Layout
*Libs to help you with layout.* [back to top](#readme) 

* [BrickKit](https://github.com/wayfair-archive/brickkit-ios) - Create complex and responsive layouts in a simple way.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wayfair-archive/brickkit-ios) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/wayfair-archive/brickkit-ios) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/wayfair-archive/brickkit-ios) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/wayfair-archive/brickkit-ios) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/wayfair-archive/brickkit-ios) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/wayfair-archive/brickkit-ios) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/wayfair-archive/brickkit-ios)

* [CGLayout](https://github.com/k-o-d-e-n/CGLayout) :penguin: - Powerful autolayout framework, that can manage UIView(NSView), CALayer, not rendered views and etc. Provides placeholders.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/k-o-d-e-n/CGLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/k-o-d-e-n/CGLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/k-o-d-e-n/CGLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/k-o-d-e-n/CGLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/k-o-d-e-n/CGLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/k-o-d-e-n/CGLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/k-o-d-e-n/CGLayout)

* [FlexLayout](https://github.com/layoutBox/FlexLayout) - Nice and clean interface to the highly optimized Facebook yoga Flexbox implementation.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/layoutBox/FlexLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/layoutBox/FlexLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/layoutBox/FlexLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/layoutBox/FlexLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/layoutBox/FlexLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/layoutBox/FlexLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/layoutBox/FlexLayout)

* [Grid](https://github.com/exyte/Grid) - The most powerful Grid container missed in SwiftUI.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/exyte/Grid) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/exyte/Grid) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/exyte/Grid) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/exyte/Grid) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/exyte/Grid) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/exyte/Grid) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/exyte/Grid)

* [LayoutKit](https://github.com/LinkedInAttic/LayoutKit) - LayoutKit is a fast view layout library for iOS, macOS, and tvOS.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LinkedInAttic/LayoutKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/LinkedInAttic/LayoutKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/LinkedInAttic/LayoutKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/LinkedInAttic/LayoutKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/LinkedInAttic/LayoutKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/LinkedInAttic/LayoutKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/LinkedInAttic/LayoutKit)

* [LayoutLess](https://github.com/DeclarativeHub/Layoutless) - Write less UI Code.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DeclarativeHub/Layoutless) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/DeclarativeHub/Layoutless) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/DeclarativeHub/Layoutless) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/DeclarativeHub/Layoutless) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/DeclarativeHub/Layoutless) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/DeclarativeHub/Layoutless) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/DeclarativeHub/Layoutless)

* [Neon](https://github.com/mamaral/Neon) - A powerful programmatic UI layout framework.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mamaral/Neon) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/mamaral/Neon) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/mamaral/Neon) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/mamaral/Neon) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/mamaral/Neon) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/mamaral/Neon) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/mamaral/Neon)

* [PinLayout](https://github.com/layoutBox/PinLayout) - Fast Views layouting without auto layout. No magic, pure code, full control and blazing fast. Concise syntax, intuitive, readable & chainable. [iOS/macOS/tvOS]

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/layoutBox/PinLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/layoutBox/PinLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/layoutBox/PinLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/layoutBox/PinLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/layoutBox/PinLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/layoutBox/PinLayout) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/layoutBox/PinLayout)

* [Scaling Header Scroll View](https://github.com/exyte/ScalingHeaderScrollView) - A scroll view with a sticky header which shrinks as you scroll. Written with SwiftUI.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/exyte/ScalingHeaderScrollView) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/exyte/ScalingHeaderScrollView) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/exyte/ScalingHeaderScrollView) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/exyte/ScalingHeaderScrollView) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/exyte/ScalingHeaderScrollView) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/exyte/ScalingHeaderScrollView) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/exyte/ScalingHeaderScrollView)

* [Static](https://github.com/venmo/Static) - A simple static table views for iOS.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/venmo/Static) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/venmo/Static) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/venmo/Static) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/venmo/Static) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/venmo/Static) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/venmo/Static) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/venmo/Static)

* [Stevia](https://github.com/freshOS/Stevia) - Elegant view layout for iOS.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/freshOS/Stevia) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/freshOS/Stevia) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/freshOS/Stevia) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/freshOS/Stevia) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/freshOS/Stevia) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/freshOS/Stevia) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/freshOS/Stevia)


#### Auto Layout
*Bored of using storyboard? Give a try to declarative auto layout libs.* [back to top](#readme) 

* [Bamboo](https://github.com/wordlessj/Bamboo) - Auto Layout (and manual layout) in one line.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wordlessj/Bamboo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/wordlessj/Bamboo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/wordlessj/Bamboo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/wordlessj/Bamboo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/wordlessj/Bamboo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/wordlessj/Bamboo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/wordlessj/Bamboo)

* [Cartography](https://github.com/robb/Cartography) - Declarative auto layout lib for your project.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/robb/Cartography) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/robb/Cartography) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/robb/Cartography) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/robb/Cartography) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/robb/Cartography) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/robb/Cartography) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/robb/Cartography)

* [Cassowary](https://github.com/tribalworldwidelondon/CassowarySwift) - A linear constraint solving library using the same algorithm as AutoLayout.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tribalworldwidelondon/CassowarySwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/tribalworldwidelondon/CassowarySwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/tribalworldwidelondon/CassowarySwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/tribalworldwidelondon/CassowarySwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/tribalworldwidelondon/CassowarySwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/tribalworldwidelondon/CassowarySwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/tribalworldwidelondon/CassowarySwift)

* [Cupcake](https://github.com/nerdycat/Cupcake) - An easy way to create and layout UI components for iOS.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tonystone/tracelog) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/tonystone/tracelog) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/tonystone/tracelog) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/tonystone/tracelog) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/tonystone/tracelog) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/tonystone/tracelog) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/tonystone/tracelog)

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wojteklu/Watchdog) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/wojteklu/Watchdog) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/wojteklu/Watchdog) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/wojteklu/Watchdog) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/wojteklu/Watchdog) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/wojteklu/Watchdog) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/wojteklu/Watchdog)

* [WatchdogInspector](https://github.com/tapwork/WatchdogInspector) - A logging tool to show the current framerate (fps) in the status bar of your iOS app.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tapwork/WatchdogInspector) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/tapwork/WatchdogInspector) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/tapwork/WatchdogInspector) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/tapwork/WatchdogInspector) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/tapwork/WatchdogInspector) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/tapwork/WatchdogInspector) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/tapwork/WatchdogInspector)

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Nike-Inc/Willow) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Nike-Inc/Willow) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/Nike-Inc/Willow) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/Nike-Inc/Willow) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/Nike-Inc/Willow) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Nike-Inc/Willow) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/Nike-Inc/Willow)

### Network
*A list of libs that allow you to decrease the amount of time spent dealing with http requests.* [back to top](#readme) 

* [Alamofire](https://github.com/Alamofire/Alamofire) :penguin: - Elegant networking.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Alamofire/Alamofire) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Alamofire/Alamofire) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/Alamofire/Alamofire) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/Alamofire/Alamofire) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/Alamofire/Alamofire) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Alamofire/Alamofire) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/Alamofire/Alamofire)

* [APIKit](https://github.com/ishkawa/APIKit) - Library for building type-safe web API client.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ishkawa/APIKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/ishkawa/APIKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/ishkawa/APIKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/ishkawa/APIKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/ishkawa/APIKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/ishkawa/APIKit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/ishkawa/APIKit)

* [Ciao](https://github.com/AlTavares/Ciao) - Publish and discover services using mDNS (Bonjour, Zeroconf).

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AlTavares/Ciao) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/AlTavares/Ciao) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/AlTavares/Ciao) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/AlTavares/Ciao) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/AlTavares/Ciao) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/AlTavares/Ciao) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/AlTavares/Ciao)

* [CodyFire](https://github.com/CodyFlame/CodyFire) - Powerful Codable API requests builder and manager for iOS. Based on Alamofire.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CodyFlame/CodyFire) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/CodyFlame/CodyFire) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/CodyFlame/CodyFire) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/CodyFlame/CodyFire) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/CodyFlame/CodyFire) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/CodyFlame/CodyFire) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/CodyFlame/CodyFire)

* [Connectivity](https://github.com/rwbutler/Connectivity) - 🌐 Makes Internet connectivity detection more robust by detecting Wi-Fi networks without Internet access.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rwbutler/Connectivity) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/rwbutler/Connectivity) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/rwbutler/Connectivity) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/rwbutler/Connectivity) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/rwbutler/Connectivity) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/rwbutler/Connectivity) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/rwbutler/Connectivity)

* [ResponseDetective](https://github.com/netguru/ResponseDetective) - A non-intrusive framework for intercepting any outgoing requests and incoming responses between your app and server for debugging purposes.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/netguru/ResponseDetective) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/netguru/ResponseDetective) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/netguru/ResponseDetective) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/netguru/ResponseDetective) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/netguru/ResponseDetective) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/netguru/ResponseDetective) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/netguru/ResponseDetective)

### PDF

#### Mock
[back to top](#readme) 

* [AutoMockable](https://github.com/vincent-pradeilles/AutoMocker) - A framework that leverages the type system to let you easily create mocked instances of your data types.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vincent-pradeilles/AutoMocker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/vincent-pradeilles/AutoMocker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/vincent-pradeilles/AutoMocker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/vincent-pradeilles/AutoMocker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/vincent-pradeilles/AutoMocker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/vincent-pradeilles/AutoMocker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/vincent-pradeilles/AutoMocker)

* [Cuckoo](https://github.com/Brightify/Cuckoo) - First boilerplate-free mocking framework.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Brightify/Cuckoo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Brightify/Cuckoo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/Brightify/Cuckoo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/Brightify/Cuckoo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/Brightify/Cuckoo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Brightify/Cuckoo) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/Brightify/Cuckoo)

* [Mocker](https://github.com/WeTransfer/Mocker) - Mock Alamofire and URLSession requests without touching your code implementation

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/WeTransfer/Mocker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/WeTransfer/Mocker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/WeTransfer/Mocker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/WeTransfer/Mocker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/WeTransfer/Mocker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/WeTransfer/Mocker) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/WeTransfer/Mocker)

* [Mockingbird](https://github.com/Farfetch/mockingbird) - Simplify software testing, by easily mocking any system using HTTP/HTTPS, allowing a team to test and develop against a service that is not complete, unstable or just to reproduce planned cases.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Farfetch/mockingbird) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/Farfetch/mockingbird) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/Farfetch/mockingbird) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/Farfetch/mockingbird) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/Farfetch/mockingbird) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Farfetch/mockingbird) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/Farfetch/mockingbird)

* [Mockingjay](https://github.com/kylef/Mockingjay) - An elegant library for stubbing HTTP requests with ease.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kylef/Mockingjay) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/kylef/Mockingjay) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/kylef/Mockingjay) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/kylef/Mockingjay) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/kylef/Mockingjay) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/kylef/Mockingjay) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/kylef/Mockingjay)

* [Mockit](https://github.com/sabirvirtuoso/Mockit) - A simple mocking framework, inspired by the famous Mockito for Java.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sabirvirtuoso/Mockit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/sabirvirtuoso/Mockit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/sabirvirtuoso/Mockit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/sabirvirtuoso/Mockit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/sabirvirtuoso/Mockit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/sabirvirtuoso/Mockit) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/sabirvirtuoso/Mockit)

* [MockSwift](https://github.com/leoture/MockSwift) - Mock Framework that uses the power of property wrappers.

   ![](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/leoture/MockSwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/leoture/MockSwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues/leoture/MockSwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/issues-pr/leoture/MockSwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/license/leoture/MockSwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/leoture/MockSwift) ![](https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/leoture/MockSwift)


### Text

#### Blur

### Utility
*Some interesting utilities to help you in your projects* [back to top](#readme) 

* [AlexaSkillsKit](https://github.com/choefele/AlexaSkillsKit) - Develop custom Alexa Skills.

### Video
[back to top](#readme) 

* [BMPlayer](https://github.com/BrikerMan/BMPlayer) - A video player for iOS, based on AVPlayer, support the horizontal, vertical screen. support adjust volume, brigtness and seek by slide.

* [NextLevelSessionExporter](https://github.com/NextLevel/NextLevelSessionExporter) - Export and transcode media.

### Contributing

Please take a quick look at the [contribution guidelines](.github/CONTRIBUTING.md) first. If you see a package or project here that is no longer maintained or is not a good fit, please submit a pull request to improve this file. Thank you to all [contributors](https://github.com/matteocrippa/awesome-swift/graphs/contributors); you rock!!
